            FROM wp_rg_lead l

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.form_id=11 AND l.status = 'active')
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,20
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

2016-07-26 20:48:09 - DEBUG --> 
            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.status = 'active' AND l.created_by = '0') AND (l.form_id=11)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,999999
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.form_id=3 AND l.status = 'active')
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,20
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.form_id=3 AND l.status = 'active')
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 2,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            INNER JOIN
            (

                (

                    FROM wp_rg_lead l

                ) page

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.form_id=3 AND l.status = 'active')
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,20
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort
